Cloud mailbox with automapped OnPremise mailbox - Microsoft Community

ari-piroozi say:

Cloud mailbox with automapped OnPremise mailbox

Hello,

One of my users had delegated access to a sharedmailbox in the onpremis envirement.

During the migration we did'nt  remove the automapping for the shared mailbox. The mailbox is now in Exchange online and the shared mailbox is onpremise.

The user is still able to see the shared mailbox in Outlook as delegated mailbox, however not able to open it.

We want to remove this sharedmailbox for this user. Is there anyway to remove the automapping for the onpremise shared mailbox.

Regards,

Ari

srijayaram say:

Automapping is unsupported in Exchange hybrid deployment.

Reference:

https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/jj906433(v=exchg.150)

Hence, it is safe to right click and remove the shared mailbox.

No handwriting recognition for Samsung Galaxy Note 10.1 2014 Edition - Microsoft Community

rauchc say:

No handwriting recognition for Samsung Galaxy Note 10.1 2014 Edition

After taking notes in OneNote for Android using my SPen on my Galaxy Note 10.1 2014 Edition I am not able to search them nor to convert them into text in OneNote 2013 on my Windows PC. Notes taken on my Galxy S4 (same App no SPen) are searchable as well as convertible. Is this a known bug?

0 people found this helpful

rauchc say:

Hello everybody,

I partly solved this: The Problem is not, that the handwriting recognition isn't working but that the handwritten notes taken on my tablet are assumed to be English (USA). On the Windows PC running OneNote handwriting recognition for English (USA) wasn't installed so the notes weren't transformed at all. Now that I installed Englisch (USA) the notes are converted. Great! ... BUT: I do not take English notes most of the time.

So next question: How can I tell OneNote for Android to process my notes like German words not English?

Spacing between references and text in Word for Mac - Microsoft Community

kilianv3 say:

Spacing between references and text in Word for Mac

Hey everyone!

I'm having troubles with the space between the normal text and the references. Before the references comes a horizontal line. And then there is a lot of wasted space between that horizontal line and the first reference. I attached a picture for better understanding.

I'm using Microsoft Word for Mac, Version 16.17

Thank you in advance :)

peter s. 1992 say:
Hi again :)

Please try the steps below.

Make sure you are viewing your document in Draft view. (Click on the Draft View icon on the status bar of the document.)
Display the References tab of the ribbon.
Click Show Notes.
If you have both footnotes and endnotes defined in your document, Word displays the View Footnotes dialog box

Click on the View Footnote Area radio button.
Click on OK.
Using the Footnotes drop-down list at the top of the Footnotes window, choose Footnote Separator. The current separator appears in the window, and the insertion point should be within the separator.
Use Word's regular formatting tools to change the paragraph indentation on the separator.
Click on Close.

Outlook for Mac version 15.32 Constantly Crashes after Upgrading to - Microsoft Community

jmdukepa say:

Outlook for Mac version 15.32 Constantly Crashes after Upgrading to Sierra

Needed to upgrade to Sierra in order to fix issues with corporate proxy.  Now, Outlook for Mac constantly crashes in the office but runs fine at home where there is no proxy.

gary zhu msft support say:

H JmdukePA,

 

According to your description, I notice the issue occurs when your Mac connects to the corporate proxy network in the office, but works fine at home. So, it might be related to your corporate proxy network or the Mac client. Since our forum focuses on Office 365 for Business online services, I recommend you contact the IT administrator of your organization to troubleshot the issue. Meanwhile, you can also contact the Apple support to get how to upgrade the OS of your Mac.

 

Thanks,

Gary 

jmdukepa say: The issue is with Outlook that constantly crashes while connected to the network in our office.  Other applications work just fine there.  There were similar issues with older versions of Outlook with the exact same thing; Outlook would continually crash.  When submitting this issue, I selected all of the categories that seemed to make sense; i do not recall anything that said 'online service' which I assume means the web portal.

gary zhu msft support say:

H JmdukePA,

 

Thanks for your quick response. Since the Outlook for Mac client crashes when connecting the office network, but works fine at your home, I’d like to confirm whether the other users in your organization have the same issue.

 

According to this article, we know Apple released Mac OS 10.12 Sierra on 9/20/2016. Some customers are reporting Office 2016 for Mac applications are closing unexpectedly, or crashing when an Office application is launched, or when the computer is moved between Wi-Fi networks. Customers in a workplace or school network configuration who wish to upgrade to Mac OS Sierra should update to Mac OS Sierra 10.12.2 or later, for improved stability specific to proxy networks.

 

Turning off “Auto Proxy Discovery” or “Automatic Proxy Configuration” is a possible workaround, if allowed by your organization’s network configuration. Here are the steps:

  1. Go to System Preferences and open Network.
  2. Click on Advanced and go to Proxies.
  3. Check if "Auto Proxy Discovery" or "Automatic Proxy Configuration" is turned on.

 

Thanks,

Gary

Excel VBA code for Default value in cell - Microsoft Community

praveen vobilisetty say:

Excel VBA code for Default value in cell

I have certain range of cells in a sheet from B37:AE39, where user should provide only date as input. and if user deletes the data then cell should have a default indication/value as  "DD-MM-YY".

I don't know coding so, I request someone to help on this issue.

hansv mvp say:

Right-click the sheet tab.

Select View Code from the context menu.

Copy the following code into the worksheet module:

Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
    Dim rng1 As Range
    Dim rng2 As Range
    On Error Resume Next
    Set rng1 = Intersect(Range("B37:AE39"), Target)
    Set rng2 = rng1.SpecialCells(xlCellTypeBlanks)
    Set rng2 = Intersect(rng1, rng2)
    If Not rng2 Is Nothing Then
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        rng2.Value = "DD-MM-YY"
        Application.EnableEvents = True
    End If
End Sub

Switch back to Excel.

Save the workbook in a macro-enabled format such as .xlsm.

Make sure that you allow macros when you open the workbook.

zach prins say:

Hi Praveen,

While in the sheet you want the defaults to be in, press Alt-F11. This will take you to the VBA editor, and the worksheet code.

Now, paste the following code into the editor window:

        

Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)

    If Not Intersect(Target, Range("B37:AE39")) Is Nothing Then

        If Target.Value = "" Then Target.Value = "DD-MM-YY"

    End If

End Sub

Every time a value is changed, we check if it was in the range B37:AE39, then we check if it was changed to a blank value. If so, we replace the blank value with DD-MM-YY.

Regards,

Zach

2. Find the following registry path and delete the affected accounts of the Office profile:HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Common\Identity\Identities

If the issue persists, to help us clarify the scenario, please provide some more information:

1. If user’s credential hasn’t been saved into the computer, it will promote user to activate Office again. Please let a user sign in and check whether the credential of the user

3. How do you deployment Office 365 Shared Computer Activation?

Regards,

Joshua

davidpaugam say:
  • uninstall Office 365
  • Edit a new .xml file for ODT deployment and add those lines:
<Property Name="SCLCacheOverride" Value="1"/>
<Property Name="SCLCacheOverrideDirectory" Value="\\srv-\share$\%username%"/>
  • install Office 365 with the new XML file
  • enable via the GPO(download the last ADMX file of Office 2016 from internet)
  • and that's it, the 2 files of the license token should now appear in your redirected folder

Hope it helps,

David

happyfunjay say: FWIW, I was encountering the same error ("phone numbers and websites can only contain English characters...") recently when trying to import my contacts from Outlook 2002 into Outlook.com.  After a fair amount of inspection and experimentation, I finally figured out the source of the problem:  I regularly use iTunes to sync my Outlook 2002 contacts with my iPhone.

I discovered that my iPhone had recently begun to store new phone numbers in my contacts with a 'ÿ' character ('y' with an umlaut).  For example:  (123)ÿ456-7890.  (Perhaps this is a bug in iOS 7; who knows.)  To further complicate matters, this bogus character would not appear in my iPhone or Outlook contact info; it just appeared as a normal space.  The characters only showed up in the csv file I exported from Outlook.  To fix it, I searched for every occurrence of the offending character in the csv file, matched it up with the contact in Outlook, and manually deleted any space characters from the corresponding phone number.  Then I re-exported the csv file, and Outlook.com happily accepted it.

Hope this helps someone.

Combo Box - Adding when Not In List is returning Data Type Conversion - Microsoft Community

nancydocken say:

Combo Box - Adding when Not In List is returning Data Type Conversion Error #3421

I'm trying to allow people to add data to a combo drop down list if the thing they are entering is not on the list. I have 5 tables that each have only two fields in my database (Books, Categories, SubCategories, Brands, and Sources). The two fields are a primary key (autonumber) and a text field.

 

The first thing you should know is that I'm trying to use Allen Browne's Not In List code. I added his Function to my General module, so it will be available to any code.

Function Append2Table(cbo As ComboBox, NewData As Variant) As Integer
On Error GoTo Err_Append2Table
' Purpose:   Append NotInList value to combo's recordset.
' Assumes:   ControlSource of combo has the same name as the foreign key field.
' Return:    acDataErrAdded if added, else acDataErrContinue
' Usage:     Add this line to the combo's NotInList event procedure:
'                Response = Append2Table(Me.MyCombo, NewData)
    Dim rst As DAO.Recordset
    Dim sMsg As String
    Dim sMsg As String
    Dim vField As Variant      ' Name of the field to append to.
    Dim vField As Variant      ' Name of the field to append to.

    Append2Table = acDataErrContinue
    Append2Table = acDataErrContinue
    vField = cbo.ControlSource
    vField = cbo.ControlSource
    If Not (IsNull(vField) Or IsNull(NewData)) Then
    If Not (IsNull(vField) Or IsNull(NewData)) Then
        sMsg = "Do you wish to add the entry " & NewData & " for " & cbo.Name & "?"
        sMsg = "Do you wish to add the entry " & NewData & " for " & cbo.Name & "?"
        If MsgBox(sMsg, vbOKCancel + vbQuestion, "Add new value?") = vbOK Then
        If MsgBox(sMsg, vbOKCancel + vbQuestion, "Add new value?") = vbOK Then
            Set rst = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset(cbo.RowSource)
            Set rst = CurrentDb.OpenRecordset(cbo.RowSource)
            rst.AddNew
            rst.AddNew
                rst(vField) = NewData
                rst(vField) = NewData
            rst.Update
            rst.Update
            rst.Close
            rst.Close
            Append2Table = acDataErrAdded
            Append2Table = acDataErrAdded
        End If
        End If
    End If
    End If

Exit_Append2Table:
    Set rst = Nothing
    Set rst = Nothing
    Exit Function
    Exit Function

Err_Append2Table:
    MsgBox "Error " & Err.Number & ": " & Err.Description, vbInformation, "Append2Table()"
    MsgBox "Error " & Err.Number & ": " & Err.Description, vbInformation, "Append2Table()"
    Resume Exit_Append2Table
    Resume Exit_Append2Table
End Function

Then I went to each of my forms (in design view) containing a combo box that I wished to make updateable. I would click on the combo box in question, make sure the combo box had a good name (Example:  cboBooks, cboCategory, cboSubCat, cboBrand, or cboSource).

 

On the Property Sheet Data tab, I made sure that the Control Source is the primary key of the table into which data will be entered, the Row Source is the query supplying this combo box, Limit to List is "Yes", Allow Value List Edits is "Yes", List Items Edit Form is set to the form where these items are normally added, and Locked is "No". Then on the Property Sheet Event tab, I selected On Not In List and selected Code.

 

When the code window opened, I added the following line immediately after the Sub line:

    

Response = Append2Table(Me![MyCombo], NewData)

I replaced MyCombo with the actual combo name as shown in the Sub line.

 

I believe I've done everything correctly, but when I try to add new data to the Books Combo (cboBooks), I keep getting "Error 3421 Data type conversion error."

 

Can anyone tell me where I've gone astray? I THINK it's possible that this is trying to enter text into the autonumber primary key field, but how do I correct that. The primary key is the only field from the Books table that I'm offered when I select the Control Source. Also, I'm not good at writing code, which is why I borrow from smart people like Allen Browne (and you guys of course.)

 

Any help is appreciated.

 

 

 

It may help you to know that in this code window, Option Explicit has been specified.

 

ken sheridan say: Looking at Allen Browne's function more closely, if I understand it rightly, where the value of the combo box is a surrogate numeric key, it would not work as it would be attempting to insert the text value of the NewData argument into the numeric primary key column.  It looks to me as though the code would only work if the keys are 'natural' not 'surrogate'.  This would explain the error which you are encountering.

If you look at the code in my demo the value is inserted into the non-key text column in the referenced table, with a value being inserted automatically into the numeric primary key column by virtue of its being an autonumber.  Amending my code so that it would insert a row into a table Books with columns BookID and BookName for instance:

Private Sub BookID_NotInList(NewData As String, Response As Integer)

    Dim ctrl As Control
    Dim strSQL As String, strMessage As String
    
    Set ctrl = Me.ActiveControl
    strMessage = "Add " & NewData & " to list?"
    
    strSQL = "INSERT INTO Books(BookName) VALUES(""" & _
            NewData & """)"
   
    If MsgBox(strMessage, vbYesNo + vbQuestion) = vbYes Then
        CurrentDb.Execute strSQL, dbFailOnError
        Response = acDataErrAdded
    Else
        Response = acDataErrContinue
        ctrl.Undo
    End If
    
End Sub

Note that in this case there is no need to open a Books form as no other data than the book name is being inserted, but where a separate form is opened then the key thing is that it is opened in dialogue mode to cause execution of the code in the calling procedure to pause until the called form is closed.

For Allen Browne's function to work in this context the name of the foreign key column in the referencing table would, as far as I can see, need to be the same as that of the non-key text column in the referenced table, i.e. BookName with the example above, but for greater clarity of the model it is usually recommended that a foreign key be given the same name as the referenced primary key.  This is not always possible, however, as more than one column could be referencing the same primary key column in a referenced table, e.g. in an adjacency list table modelling a bill of materials, where it would be appropriate to name the columns to indicate the function, e.g. MajorPartID and MinorPartID, both referencing the primary key PartID of a Parts table.

alex chen msft say:

Hi Sofia,

 

Thanks for your query in this community.

To address your first question:

Unlike the SharePoint Team Site, when you create a Communication Site, it won't automatically generate an Office 365 Group with it. But you can manually add an existing Office 365 Group to the Site as Site Members. Communication sites are meant to have a relatively smaller set of editors and a large amount of readers. We are sorry about the inconvenience caused by this. If you are expecting on team collaboration, we would kindly suggest you create a Team Site instead.

 

About your second concern, temporary SharePoint Server Publishing  Infrastructure is not avail in Modern Communication Site. Given this situation, we would kindly recommend you vote the following idea.

 In SPO, enable the option of activating SP publishing infrastructure feature in Communication sites

Your understanding is highly appreciated.

 

Regards,

Alex Chen
